1  Mengambil daftar stopword dari NLTK

import requests as req
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup as bs
from datetime import datetime
import csv

hades = {'user-agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/68.0.3440.106 Safari/537.36'}
def scrape_detik(hal):
  global hades
  a = 1
  for page in range(1,hal):
    url = f'https://www.detik.com/search/searchall?query=pariwisata&sortby=time&page={page}'
    ge = req.get(url,hades).text
    sop = bs(ge,'lxml')
    li = sop.find('div',class_='list media_rows list-berita')
    lin = li.find_all('article')
    for x in lin:
            link = x.find('a')['href']
            date = x.find('a').find('span',class_='date').text.replace('WIB','').replace('detikNews','').split(',')[1]
            headline = x.find('a').find('h2').text
            ge_ = req.get(link,hades).text
            sop_ = bs(ge_,'lxml')
            content = sop_.find_all('div',class_='detail__body-text itp_bodycontent')
            for x in content:
                x = x.find_all('p')
                y  = [y.text for y in x ]
                content_ = ''.join(y).replace('\n', '').replace('ADVERTISEMENT','').replace('SCROLL TO RESUME CONTENT','')
                print(f'done[{a}] > {headline[0:10]}')
                a += 1
                with open('Data_Coba1.csv','a')as file:
                    wr = csv.writer(file, delimiter=',')
                    wr.writerow([headline,date,link,content_])
scrape_detik(2)

import re
def cleaning(data):
  data = re.sub(r"_x000d_",'',data)
  data = re.sub(r'#[A-Za-z0-9]+',' ',data)
  data = re.sub(r"http\S+",' ',data)
  data = re.sub(r'[0-9]+',' ',data)
  data = re.sub(r"[-()\"#/@;:<>{}'+=~|%!?,_]", " ", data)
  data = data.strip("")
  data = data.strip("\n")

  return data

df["cleaning"]= df["casefolding"].apply(cleaning)
df.head()

import nltk
nltk.download('punkt')
def split_paragraph_into_sentences(paragraph):
    sentences = nltk.sent_tokenize(paragraph)
    return sentences
df["tokenize"] = df["cleaning"].apply(split_paragraph_into_sentences)

import nltk
nltk.download('stopwords')
from nltk.corpus import stopwords

daftar_stopword_nltk = stopwords.words('indonesian')
# daftar_stopword1 = ["web","teknologi"]
data_stopword1 = input(str("Masukkan kata :"))
data_stopword1 = re.sub(r",",' ',data_stopword1)
data_split = data_stopword1.split()
data_split

# Menggabungkan kedua daftar stopword
daftar_stopword = data_split + daftar_stopword_nltk
[nltk_data] Downloading package stopwords to /root/nltk_data...
[nltk_data]   Unzipping corpora/stopwords.zip.
Masukkan kata :
def remove_stopwords(sentence):
    words = nltk.word_tokenize(sentence)
    filtered_words = [word for word in words if word.lower() not in daftar_stopword]
    return ' '.join(filtered_words)

# Menghapus stopword dari kolom 'tokenize'
df['Stopword'] = df['tokenize'].apply(lambda sentences: [remove_stopwords(sentence) for sentence in sentences])

df

def remove_period_from_list(lst):
    return [word.replace(".", "") for word in lst]

# Menghapus tanda titik dari kolom 'tokenize'
for i in range(len(df["Stopword"])):
    df["Stopword"][i] = remove_period_from_list(df["Stopword"][i])
df

from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer

# Data korpus
corpus = df["Stopword"]

# Menggabungkan list dalam korpus menjadi kalimat
corpus = [' '.join(doc) for doc in corpus]

# Membuat objek TfidfVectorizer
tfidf_vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()

# Menghitung TF-IDF dari korpus
tfidf_matrix = tfidf_vectorizer.fit_transform(corpus)

# Membuat DataFrame Pandas dari matriks TF-IDF
tfidf_df = pd.DataFrame(tfidf_matrix.toarray(), columns=tfidf_vectorizer.get_feature_names_out())

# Menampilkan DataFrame
tfidf_df

from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity

# Menghitung cosine similarity antara dokumen dalam matriks TF-IDF
cosine_sim = cosine_similarity(tfidf_matrix, tfidf_matrix)

# Membuat DataFrame Pandas dari matriks cosine similarity
cosine_sim_df = pd.DataFrame(cosine_sim, index=df.index, columns=df.index)

import networkx as nx
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

# Membuat objek Graph dari matriks cosine similarity
G = nx.Graph()

# Menambahkan simpul (nodes) ke grafik
for i in range(len(cosine_sim_df.index)):
    G.add_node(i)

# Menambahkan tepian (edges) berdasarkan nilai cosine similarity
for i in range(len(cosine_sim_df.index)):
    for j in range(i + 1, len(cosine_sim_df.index)):
        similarity = cosine_sim_df.iloc[i, j]
        if similarity > 0.7:
            G.add_edge(i, j, weight=similarity)

# Mengatur posisi simpul dalam grafik
pos = nx.spring_layout(G)

# Menggambar grafik
plt.figure(figsize=(10, 10))
nx.draw(G, pos, with_labels=True, node_size=200, font_size=8)

# Menambahkan label edge berdasarkan similarity
labels = nx.get_edge_attributes(G, 'weight')
nx.draw_networkx_edge_labels(G, pos, edge_labels=labels)

# Menampilkan grafik
plt.show()

import pandas as pd

# Menghitung closeness centrality
closeness_centrality = nx.closeness_centrality(G, distance='weight')

# Membuat DataFrame Pandas dari closeness centrality
closeness_centrality_df = pd.DataFrame(list(closeness_centrality.items()), columns=['Simpul', 'Closeness Centrality'])

# Menampilkan DataFrame closeness centrality
closeness_centrality_df

import pandas as pd
import networkx as nx

# Menghitung closeness centrality
closeness_centrality = nx.closeness_centrality(G, distance='weight')

# Membuat DataFrame Pandas dari closeness centrality
closeness_centrality_df = pd.DataFrame(list(closeness_centrality.items()), columns=['Simpul', 'Closeness Centrality'])

# Mengurutkan DataFrame berdasarkan Closeness Centrality terkecil hingga terbesar
sorted_closeness_centrality_df = closeness_centrality_df.sort_values(by='Closeness Centrality')

print("DataFrame Closeness Centrality (Terurut):")
for index, row in sorted_closeness_centrality_df.iterrows():
    node = row['Simpul']
    centrality = row['Closeness Centrality']
    kalimat = df["Stopword"][node]  # Ganti 'sentences' dengan data kalimat Anda
    print(f"Simpul {node}: Closeness Centrality = {centrality:.4f}, Kalimat: {kalimat}")

import networkx as nx
import pandas as pd

# Menghitung Eigenvector Centrality
eigenvector_centrality = nx.eigenvector_centrality(G)

# Membuat DataFrame Pandas dari Eigenvector Centrality

# Mengurutkan DataFrame berdasarkan Eigenvector Centrality terbesar ke terkecil

from sumy.summarizers.lex_rank import LexRankSummarizer
import nltk
nltk.download('punkt')
# Fungsi untuk mengekstrak kalimat penting dari dokumen menggunakan Sumy
def extract_important_sentence(doc_text):
    # Menggunakan Sumy untuk ekstraksi kalimat penting
    language = "indonesian"
    parser = PlaintextParser.from_string(doc_text, Tokenizer(language))
    summarizer = LexRankSummarizer()
    sentences = summarizer(parser.document, 1)
    important_sentence = str(sentences[0])
    return important_sentence

# Menambahkan kolom "Kalimat Penting" ke DataFrame
page_rank_df['Kalimat Penting'] = [extract_important_sentence(' '.join(corpus[doc_index])) for doc_index in page_rank_df['Dokumen']]

# Menampilkan DataFrame dengan kolom "Kalimat Penting"
print(page_rank_df)
